# Fraction Addition: Same Denominator

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Adding and Subtracting Fractions with the Same Denominator**  |
+===================================================================+
| When working with fractions that have the same denominator:       |
|                                                                   |
| 1.  Add or subtract the numerators.                               |
|                                                                   |
| 2.  The denominators stay the same.                               |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - ![](media/image2.png){width="0.5833333333333334in"                                    |
|   height="0.40208333333333335in"}![](media/image3.png){width="0.5833333333333334in"     |
|   height="0.4083333333333333in"}![](media/image4.png){width="2.178472222222222in"       |
|   height="0.4388888888888889in"}![](media/image4.png){width="2.178472222222222in"       |
|   height="0.4388888888888889in"}**Example** Add and subtract fractions with the same    |
|   denominator                                                                           |
+============================================+============================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{2}{8} + \frac{5}{8}$$    | $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{5}{6} - \frac{2}{6}$$    |
|                                            |                                            |
| $$= \frac{7}{8}$$                          | $$= \frac{3}{6}$$                          |
+--------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                                                                                         |
+======================================================================================+========================================================================================+
| Add and subtract these fractions.                                                                                                                                             |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| a.  ![Diagram Description automatically                                              | b.  ![Diagram Description automatically generated](media/image5.png){width="0.8125in"  |
|     generated](media/image5.png){width="2.157638888888889in"                         |     height="0.44166666666666665in"}![](media/image6.png){width="0.8003040244969379in"  |
|     height="0.4388888888888889in"}![Diagram Description automatically                |     height="0.4166666666666667in"}                                                     |
|     generated](media/image5.png){width="0.8125in" height="0.44201443569553805in"}    |                                                                                        |
|                                                                                      | $$\ \ \ \ \frac{3}{4} - \frac{2}{4}$$                                                  |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{4} + \frac{2}{4}$$                                              |                                                                                        |
|                                                                                      | $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ \ }$$                                                  |
| $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ }{4}$$                                                           |                                                                                        |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| c.  ![](media/image7.png){width="0.7770833333333333in"                               | d.  ![](media/image9.png){width="0.7479166666666667in"                                 |
|     height="0.42083333333333334in"}![](media/image8.png){width="2.252083333333333in" |     height="0.38819444444444445in"}![](media/image10.png){width="0.7677165354330708in" |
|     height="0.47638888888888886in"}                                                  |     height="0.39635608048993876in"}                                                    |
|                                                                                      |                                                                                        |
| $$\ \ \ \ \frac{2}{6} + \frac{4}{6}$$                                                | $$\ \ \ \ \frac{4}{5} - \frac{1}{5}$$                                                  |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| e.                                                                                   | f.  ![A picture containing text, sky, traffic, light Description automatically         |
|                                                                                      |     generated](media/image11.png){width="2.375in" height="0.6465277777777778in"}![A    |
| $$\ \ \ \ \frac{2}{6} + \frac{3}{6}$$                                                |     picture containing text, sky, traffic, light Description automatically             |
|                                                                                      |     generated](media/image11.png){width="2.375in" height="0.6469608486439196in"}       |
|                                                                                      |                                                                                        |
|                                                                                      | $$\ \ \ \ \frac{4}{5} - \frac{3}{5}$$                                                  |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Adding and Subtracting Fractions with the Same Denominator**                                                                                                              |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| $$\frac{a}{n} + \frac{b}{n} = \frac{a + b}{n}$$                                      | $$\frac{a}{n} - \frac{b}{n} = \frac{a - b}{n}$$                                        |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - Always simplify the result, if possible.                                                                                                                                    |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Add and subtract fractions with the same denominator              |
+=========================================+=======================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{2}{5} + \frac{6}{5}$$ | $$\ \ \ \frac{9}{12} - \frac{5}{12}$$ |
|                                         |                                       |
| $$= \frac{8}{5}$$                       | $$= \frac{4}{12}$$                    |
|                                         |                                       |
|                                         | $$= \ \frac{1}{3}$$                   |
+-----------------------------------------+---------------------------------------+

+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                          |
+==============================================+=================================================+
| Add and subtract these fractions.                                                              |
+----------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------+
| a.                                           | b.                                              |
|                                              |                                                 |
| > $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{12}{19} + \frac{5}{19}$$ | > $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{9}{11} - \frac{8}{11}$$     |
| >                                            | >                                               |
| > $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{19}$$              | > $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ \ }$$       |
+----------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------+
| c.                                           | d.                                              |
|                                              |                                                 |
| > $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{9}{28} + \frac{17}{28}$$ | > $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{12}{22} - \frac{16}{22}$$ |
+----------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Key Ideas**                                                   |
+===================================================================+
| 1.  When adding or subtracting fractions with the same            |
|     denominator, we add or subtract the ........................  |
|     and keep the ........................ the same.               |
|                                                                   |
| 2.  The denominator stays the same because the ............ of    |
|     the parts stays the same.                                     |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

Foundation

|                                                                                         |                                                                                         |                                                                                               |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{4}\ \ \ \ \  + \ \ \ \ \frac{2}{4}\ \ \ \ \ \ \  =$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{4}{8}\ \ \ \ \  + \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{8}\ \ \ \ \ \ \  =$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{3}{5}\ \ \ \ \  + \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{5}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \  =$$ |

|                                                                                         |                                                                                         |                                                                                               |
| $$\frac{9}{12} = \frac{3}{4}$$                                                          | $$\frac{5}{7}$$                                                                         | $$\frac{9}{12} = \frac{3}{4}$$                                                                |

![](media/image23.png)

8.  Beca and Ed each have a piece of ribbon.\
    Beca's ribbon is $\frac{2}{7}$ of a metre.

Ed's ribbon is $\frac{5}{7}$ of a metre.

What is the total length of their ribbon?

1 m

9.  ![](media/image24.png){width="2.6319444444444446in"
    height="1.2195034995625547in"}Ed has a piece of ribbon that is a
    metre long.\
    He cuts off $\frac{3}{8}$ of a metre and gives it to Beca.\
    How much ribbon does he have left?

$$\frac{5}{8}\ m$$

10. Emily and Marta each have a piece of ribbon.\
    Emily's piece is $\frac{3}{11}$ of a metre and Marta's piece is
    $\frac{2}{11}$ of a metre.\
    What fraction of a metre of ribbon do Emily and Marta have in total?

$$\frac{5}{11}\ m$$

11. Ali is $\frac{4}{26}$ of his way through a journey. What fraction of
    the journey does he have left?

$$\frac{11}{13}$$

12. Ed, Marta and Jakub are sharing a large pizza.

Ed eats $\frac{2}{9}$ of the pizza.

Marta eats $\frac{2}{9}$ of the pizza.

Jakub eats $\frac{4}{9}$ of the pizza.

What fraction of the whole pizza did they eat?

$$\frac{8}{9}$$

What fraction of the whole pizza is left?

$$\frac{1}{9}$$

13. Ed eats $\frac{1}{9}$ of a cake. Flo eats $\frac{4}{9}$ of the same
    cake. What fraction of the cake is left?

$$\frac{4}{9}$$

14. Consider this equation:

$$\frac{2}{w} + \frac{a}{w} = \frac{9}{w}$$

a.  Work out the value of $a$

$$7$$

b.  Explain why the value of $w\$doesn't matter.

All the denominators are the same, so we only add the numerators.

c.  $w$ is a positive integer. For what values of $w$ is $\frac{9}{w}$
    an improper fraction?

3, 6, 9

|                      |                      |                      |
| $$\frac{3}{4}$$      | $$\frac{2}{5}$$      | $$\frac{3}{5}$$      |
+======================+======================+======================+
| d.  $1 =$ ...... $+$ | e.  $\frac{12}{19}$  | f.  $1 =$ ...... $-$ |
|     $\frac{3}{5}$    |     $+$ ...... $= 1$ |     $\frac{5}{7}$    |
|                      |                      |                      |
| $$\frac{2}{5}$$      | $$\frac{7}{19}$$     | $$\frac{12}{7}$$     |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| g.  $\frac{2}{7}$    | h.  $3 =$ ...... $+$ | i.  $\frac{14}{3}$   |
|     $+$ ...... $= 2$ |     $\frac{5}{9}$    |     $-$ ...... $= 4$ |
|                      |                      |                      |

+=========================================================+=========================================================+=========================================================+

# Fraction Addition: Related Denominator

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Adding and Subtracting Fractions with Related Denominators**  |
+===================================================================+
| When working with fractions that have related denominators:       |
|                                                                   |
| 1.  Rewrite the fractions with the lowest common multiple of the  |
|     denominators.                                                 |
|                                                                   |
| 2.  Add or subtract the numerators.                               |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Add and subtract fractions with related denominators                                       |
+====================================================+=====================================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \frac{1}{4} + \frac{3}{8}$$              | $$\ \ \ \ \frac{5}{12}\  - \ \frac{1}{4}$$          |
|                                                    |                                                     |
| $$= \frac{2}{8} + \frac{3}{8}$$                    | $$= \frac{5}{12} - \frac{3}{12}$$                   |
|                                                    |                                                     |
| $$= \frac{5}{8}$$                                  | $$= \frac{2}{12}$$                                  |
|                                                    |                                                     |
| ![](media/image26.png){width="2.064583333333333in" | ![](media/image27.png){width="1.9916666666666667in" |
| height="1.5972222222222223in"}                     | height="1.625in"}                                   |
+----------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                                                                 |
+===========================================================================+===========================================================================+
| Add and subtract these fractions.                                                                                                                     |
+---------------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| a.  ![A picture containing crossword puzzle, clipart Description          | b.  ![](media/image29.png){width="2.014815179352581in"                    |
|     automatically generated](media/image28.png){width="1.94375in"         |     height="1.656936789151356in"}                                         |
|     height="1.5034722222222223in"}                                        |                                                                           |
|                                                                           | $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{7}{10} - \ \frac{2}{5}$$                                |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{3}\  + \frac{1}{6}$$                                 |                                                                           |
|                                                                           | $$= \frac{7}{10} - \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{10}$$                              |
| $$= \frac{\ }{6} + \frac{1}{6}$$                                          |                                                                           |
|                                                                           | $$=$$                                                                     |
| $$=$$                                                                     |                                                                           |
+---------------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| c.  ![A picture containing text, clock Description automatically          | d.  ![Diagram Description automatically                                   |
|     generated](media/image30.png){width="0.7513888888888889in"            |     generated](media/image31.png){width="0.8054352580927384in"            |
|     height="0.49027777777777776in"}![A picture containing text, clock     |     height="0.5763888888888888in"}![Diagram Description automatically     |
|     Description automatically                                             |     generated](media/image31.png){width="1.8359383202099737in"            |
|     generated](media/image30.png){width="1.8555555555555556in"            |     height="0.5766218285214348in"}![Diagram Description automatically     |
|     height="0.49027777777777776in"}![A picture containing text, clock     |     generated](media/image31.png){width="1.8354166666666667in"            |
|     Description automatically                                             |     height="0.5763888888888888in"}                                        |
|     generated](media/image30.png){width="1.8555555555555556in"            |                                                                           |
|     height="0.49027777777777776in"}                                       | $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{2} - \ \frac{1}{4}$$                                 |
|                                                                           |                                                                           |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{3}{6}\  + \frac{1}{3}$$                                 | $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ \ } - \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ }$$ |
|                                                                           |                                                                           |
| $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ \ } + \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ \ }$$ | $$=$$                                                                     |
|                                                                           |                                                                           |
| $$=$$                                                                     |                                                                           |
+---------------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Add and subtract fractions with related denominators                                                                                                                   |
+==================================================================================================================================================+===================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{5}\  + \ \frac{3}{10}$$ | To add and subtract fractions,    |
|                                                                                                                                                  | the ........................ must |
| 1\. Same denominators $\frac{2}{10}$ $+$ $\frac{3}{10}$                                                                                          | be the same.                      |
|                                                                                                                                                  |                                   |
| 2\. Add numerators $\frac{5}{10}$                                                                                                                | We make the denominators the      |
|                                                                                                                                                  | l...............                  |
|                                                                                                                                                  | c.....................            |
|                                                                                                                                                  | m..................... by         |
|                                                                                                                                                  | multiplying the numerator and     |
|                                                                                                                                                  | denominator by the                |
|                                                                                                                                                  | ........................ number.  |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+                                   |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{9}{12}\  - \ \frac{5}{6}$$     |                                   |
|                                                                                                                                                  |                                   |
| 1\. Same denominators $\frac{9}{12}$ $-$ $\frac{10}{12}$                                                                                         |                                   |
|                                                                                                                                                  |                                   |
| 2\. Subtract numerators $-$ $\frac{1}{12}$                                                                                                       |                                   |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                                         |
+=======================================================================+=======================================================+
| Add and subtract these fractions.                                                                                             |
+-----------------------------------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------------+
| a.                                                                    | b.                                                    |
|                                                                       |                                                       |
| > $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{2}{3} + \frac{1}{9}$$                             | > $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{17}{20} - \frac{3}{5}$$           |
| >                                                                     | >                                                     |
| > $$= \frac{\ }{9} + \frac{1}{9}$$                                    | > $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ }{20} - \frac{\ \ \ \ \ }{20}$$ |
| >                                                                     | >                                                     |
| > $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ }{9}$$                                          | > $$=$$                                               |
+-----------------------------------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------------+
| c.                                                                    | d.                                                    |
|                                                                       |                                                       |
| > $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{3}{4} + \frac{5}{12}$$                            | > $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{8}{6} - \frac{5}{36}$$            |
| >                                                                     | >                                                     |
| > $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ } + \frac{\ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ }$$ | > $$=$$                                               |
| >                                                                     | >                                                     |
| > $$=$$                                                               | > $$=$$                                               |
+-----------------------------------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Key Ideas**                                                   |
+===================================================================+
| 1.  To add and subtract fractions, their                          |
|     ........................... must be the same.                 |
|                                                                   |
| 2.  If two fractions don't have the same denominator, we should   |
|     change their denominators to a common .....................   |
|                                                                   |
| 3.  To change denominators of fractions, we                       |
|     ........................ the numerator and denominator by the |
|     same number.                                                  |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

4.  Read the example carefully and answer the questions.

+-----------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------+
| ![](media/image41.png){width="2.7030927384076993in" | ![](media/image42.png){width="3.1493055555555554in" |
| height="2.7889960629921258in"}                      | height="0.8104166666666667in"}Add $\frac{1}{8}$ to  |
|                                                     | $\frac{1}{4}$ represented on the diagram below by   |
|                                                     | shading                                             |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | ![](media/image43.png){width="3.1496062992125986in" |
|                                                     | height="0.6465748031496062in"}Shade $\frac{2}{12}$  |
|                                                     | on the diagram below                                |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | Compare the two diagrams to explain why\            |
|                                                     | $\frac{1}{4} + \frac{1}{8}$ is not equal to         |
|                                                     | $\frac{2}{12}$                                      |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | Hence solve $\frac{6}{12} + \frac{2}{6}$            |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | $$\frac{5}{6}$$                                     |
+=====================================================+=====================================================+
| ![](media/image44.png){width="3.214015748031496in"  | Look at the step marked with an arrow. Why did Nate |
| height="4.039772528433946in"}                       | rewrite the first fraction as $\frac{60}{100}$?     |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | *The common ............... of 10 and 100 is        |
|                                                     | .........*                                          |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | Denominator, 100                                    |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | How do you know $\frac{6}{10}$ is equivalent to     |
|                                                     | $\frac{60}{100}$?                                   |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | *We multiply the numerator and denominator by       |
|                                                     | .........*                                          |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | 10                                                  |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | Hence solve:                                        |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | $$\frac{5}{10} + \frac{7}{100}$$                    |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | $$\frac{57}{10}$$                                   |
+-----------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------+
| ![](media/image45.png){width="3.1493055555555554in" | Explain why Jing's final answer, 0.113, is not      |
| height="3.020138888888889in"}                       | equivalent to $\frac{113}{100}$                     |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | 0.113 is less than one whole $\frac{113}{100}$ is   |
|                                                     | more than one whole                                 |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | In the step marked with an arrow, look at the       |
|                                                     | values of the numerator and the denominator. How    |
|                                                     | could Jing have known the answer should be greater  |
|                                                     | than 1?                                             |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | The numerator is greater than the denominator, so   |
|                                                     | the decimal must be greater than one.               |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | Solve. Write your answer as a decimal.              |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | $$\frac{4}{10} + \frac{95}{100}$$                   |
|                                                     |                                                     |
|                                                     | 1.35                                                |
+-----------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------+

**Development**

5.  Add these fractions.

+-------------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------------+
| a.  $\frac{3}{5} + \frac{2}{5}$                 | b.  $\frac{3}{5} - \frac{2}{5}$                 | c.  $\frac{3}{5} + \frac{3}{5} + \frac{2}{15}$ |
|                                                 |                                                 |                                                |
| $$1$$                                           | $$\frac{1}{5}$$                                 | $$\frac{4}{3}$$                                |
+=================================================+=================================================+================================================+
| d.  $\frac{7}{20} + \frac{5}{10}$               | e.  $\frac{7}{8} - \frac{3}{4}$                 | f.  $\frac{5}{6} - \frac{1}{3}$                |
|                                                 |                                                 |                                                |
| $$\frac{17}{20}$$                               | $$\frac{1}{8}$$                                 | $$\frac{1}{2}$$                                |
+-------------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------------+
| g.  $\frac{1}{4} + \frac{3}{8}$                 | h.  $\frac{2}{5} + \frac{4}{15}$                | i.  $\frac{7}{10} - \frac{2}{5}$               |
|                                                 |                                                 |                                                |
| $$\frac{5}{8}$$                                 | $$\frac{2}{3}$$                                 | $$\frac{3}{10}$$                               |
+-------------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------------+
| j.  $\frac{11}{12} - \frac{1}{3} - \frac{1}{4}$ | k.  $\frac{1}{5} + \frac{3}{10} + \frac{2}{15}$ | l.  $\frac{1}{3} + \frac{5}{12} - \frac{1}{6}$ |
|                                                 |                                                 |                                                |
| $$\frac{1}{3}$$                                 | $$\frac{19}{30}$$                               | $$\frac{7}{12}$$                               |
+-------------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------------+

6.  Chloe eats $\frac{1}{10}$ of her birthday cake. She gives her
    friends $\frac{3}{5}$ of the cake.\
    She gives her family $\frac{3}{10}$ of the cake. Does Chloe have any
    cake left?

No cake left :(

7.  Beca has some football cards.\
    She gives $\frac{1}{8}$ of them to her friend Benji and
    $\frac{1}{2}$ of them to her friend Becky.\
    What fraction of the cards does Beca have left?

$$\frac{3}{8}$$

**Mastery**

8.  Marta has a chocolate bar. She eats $\frac{2}{3}$ of the chocolate
    bar and gives her friend $\frac{1}{6}$ of it.

    a.  What fraction of the chocolate bar is eaten?

$$\frac{5}{6}$$

b.  What fraction of the chocolate bar is left?

$$\frac{1}{6}$$

9.  Jakub cycles $1$ $\frac{3}{4}$ km on Monday, and $2$ $\frac{1}{8}$
    km on Tuesday. How far does he cycle in total?

$$\frac{31}{8}$$

10. A barrel holds $12$ $\frac{1}{4}$ litres of water. A bucket holds
    $3$ $\frac{11}{12}$ litres of water.\
    Max fills up the bucket with water from the barrel. How much water
    is left in the barrel?

$$8\frac{1}{3}$$

# Fraction Addition: Unrelated Denominators

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Adding and Subtracting Fractions with Unrelated               |
|   Denominators**                                                  |
+===================================================================+
| When working with fractions that have different denominators:     |
|                                                                   |
| 1.  Rewrite the fractions with the lowest common multiple of the  |
|     denominators.                                                 |
|                                                                   |
| 2.  Add or subtract the numerators.                               |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - ![](media/image46.png){width="1.9916666666666667in"                                       |
|   height="1.6131944444444444in"}**Example** Add and subtract fractions with unrelated       |
|   denominators                                                                              |
+=====================================================+=======================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{4}{5}\  - \ \ \frac{1}{3}$$     | $$\ \ \ \ \frac{1}{2} + \frac{1}{3}$$ |
|                                                     |                                       |
| $$= \frac{12}{15} - \frac{5}{15}$$                  | $$= \frac{3}{6} + \frac{2}{6}$$       |
|                                                     |                                       |
| $$= \frac{7}{15}$$                                  | $$= \frac{5}{6}$$                     |
|                                                     |                                       |
| ![](media/image47.png){width="1.9708333333333334in" |                                       |
| height="1.5972222222222223in"}                      |                                       |
+-----------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                                                           |
+=======================================================================================+=========================================================+
| Add and subtract these fractions.                                                                                                               |
+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------+
| a.  ![](media/image48.png){width="1.9165879265091863in" height="0.9875in"}            | b.  ![](media/image49.png){width="1.9333333333333333in" |
|                                                                                       |     height="0.9656091426071741in"}                      |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{5}\  + \frac{2}{3}$$                                             |                                                         |
|                                                                                       | $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{2} - \ \frac{2}{7}$$               |
| $$= \frac{}{15} + \frac{}{15}$$                                                       |                                                         |
|                                                                                       | $$= \frac{}{14} - \frac{}{14}$$                         |
| $$= \frac{}{}$$                                                                       |                                                         |
|                                                                                       | $$= \frac{}{}$$                                         |
+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------+
| c.  ![](media/image50.png){width="1.4131944444444444in"                               | d.  ![](media/image52.png){width="1.6250535870516185in" |
|     height="0.6631944444444444in"}![](media/image51.png){width="1.4326388888888888in" |     height="0.7166666666666667in"}                      |
|     height="0.6895909886264217in"}                                                    |                                                         |
|                                                                                       | $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{2}{5} - \frac{1}{3}$$               |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{2}{3} + \frac{2}{4}                                               |                                                         |
| $$                                                                                    | ![](media/image53.png){width="1.55625in"                |
|                                                                                       | height="0.6875in"}\                                     |
| $$= \frac{}{} + \frac{}{}$$                                                           | $$= \frac{}{} - \frac{}{}$$                             |
|                                                                                       |                                                         |
| $$=$$                                                                                 | $$=$$                                                   |
+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Add and subtract fractions with unrelated denominators                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
+=============================================================================================================================================================+===========================================================================================================================================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{5}\  + \ \frac{3}{4}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{9}{5}\  - \ \frac{5}{7}$$ |
|                                                                                                                                                             |                                                                                                                                                           |
| 1\. Same denominators $\frac{}{20}$ $+$ $\frac{}{20}$                                                                                                       | 1\. Same denominators $\frac{}{35}$ $-$ $\frac{}{35}$                                                                                                     |
|                                                                                                                                                             |                                                                                                                                                           |
| $\frac{4}{20}$ $+$ $\frac{15}{20}$                                                                                                                          | $\frac{63}{35}$ $-$ $\frac{25}{35}$                                                                                                                       |
|                                                                                                                                                             |                                                                                                                                                           |
| 2\. Add numerators $\frac{19}{20}$                                                                                                                          | 2\. Subtract numerators $\frac{38}{35}$                                                                                                                   |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
+===============================================+=================================================+=============================================================================+=============================================================================+
| Add and subtract these fractions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
+-----------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| a.                                            | b.                                              | c.                                                                          | d.                                                                          |
|                                               |                                                 |                                                                             |                                                                             |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{4}\ \  + \ \frac{1}{3}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{5}{4}\ \  - \ \frac{6}{7}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{3}{7}\  + \ \frac{2}{5}$$                                 | $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{7}{6}\  - \ \frac{2}{3}$$                                 |
|                                               |                                                 |                                                                             |                                                                             |
| $$= \frac{\ }{12} + \frac{\ }{12}$$           | $$= \frac{\ }{28} - \frac{\ }{28}$$             | $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ \ } + \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ \ }$$ | $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ \ } - \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ \ }$$ |
|                                               |                                                 |                                                                             |                                                                             |
| $$= \frac{\ }{12}$$                           | $$= \frac{\ }{28}$$                             | $$=$$                                                                       | $$=$$                                                                       |
+-----------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Key Ideas**                                                   |
+===================================================================+
| 1.  To add or subtract fractions, the ..................... must  |
|     be the same.                                                  |
|                                                                   |
| 2.  To make the denominators the same, determine a                |
|     ..................... ..................... of the two        |
|     denominators.                                                 |
|                                                                   |
| 3.  A quick way to make the denominators the same is to multiply  |
|     the numerator and denominator of each fraction by the         |
|     ..................... of the other.                           |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

2.  Read Yetta's work carefully and answer the questions.

+-----------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------+
| ![](media/image66.png){width="3.1493055555555554in" | What did Yetta do wrong while   |
| height="1.9236111111111112in"}                      | adding the fractions?           |
|                                                     |                                 |
|                                                     | She added the numerator and     |
|                                                     | denominator, which you can't    |
|                                                     | do.                             |
|                                                     |                                 |
|                                                     | You must make the denominators  |
|                                                     | the same.                       |
|                                                     |                                 |
|                                                     | Is Yetta's answer bigger or     |
|                                                     | smaller than the correct        |
|                                                     | answer? How can you tell?       |
|                                                     |                                 |
|                                                     | Smaller. Five-ninths is less    |
|                                                     | than three-quarters, the answer |
|                                                     | should be greater than          |
|                                                     | three-quarters                  |
+=====================================================+=================================+

7.  A survey of Year 7 students' favourite sport is carried out.\
    One fifth reply that netball is their favourite, one-quarter rugby
    and one-third soccer.\
    The remainder of students leave the question unanswered.

    a.  What fraction of the Year 7 students answered the survey
        question?

$$\frac{47}{60}$$

b.  What fraction of the Year 7 students left the question unanswered?

$$\frac{13}{60}$$

**Mastery**

8.  Seb reads $\frac{5}{36}$ of his book on Monday.

> He reads $\frac{1}{9}$ of his book on Tuesday.
>
> He reads $\frac{1}{6}$ of his book on Wednesday.
>
> He reads the rest over the weekend.
>
> How much of the book did he read over the weekend?

$$\frac{7}{12}$$

9.  Work out

$$\frac{3}{7} + \frac{4}{13} + \frac{5}{8} + \frac{9}{13} + \frac{4}{7} + \frac{1}{8}$$

Explain the most efficient method.

Do operators with fractions that have like numerators. The answer is $2$
$\frac{3}{4}$.

11. A runner covered $\frac{5}{9}$ of a marathon in 2 hours, then
    $\frac{1}{8}$ in half an hour.\
    What fraction of the course has he covered?

$$\frac{49}{72}$$

12. A farmer sold $\frac{1}{3}$ of her cows then sent $\frac{2}{5}$ to
    another ranch for the winter.\
    What fraction of her herd is *left*?

$$\frac{4}{15}$$

13. Two milk bottles are partially filled. Both milk bottles can hold
    0.9 litres.\
    One bottle is $\frac{3}{8}$ full and the other is $\frac{5}{12}$
    full.\
    Is it possible to combine the two partially filled bottles into a
    single bottle without overflowing?

$$\frac{3}{8} + \frac{5}{12} = \frac{19}{24}$$

Yes, they can fit into a single bottle

14. There is a bag of sugar in a storage room. The bag contained
    $\frac{9}{10}$ kilograms of sugar.\
    The chef filled up a can with $\frac{1}{8}$ kilogram of sugar then
    used $\frac{3}{5}$ of a kilogram of sugar for cake. How much sugar
    was left in the bag?

$$\frac{7}{40}$$

# Fraction Addition: Mixed Numbers

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Adding and Subtracting Mixed Numbers**                        |
+===================================================================+
| 1.  Convert mixed numbers to improper fractions using the rule:   |
|                                                                   |
| > $$a\frac{b}{n} = \frac{a \times n + b}{n}$$                     |
|                                                                   |
| 2.  Make the denominators the same.                               |
|                                                                   |
| 3.  Add or subtract the numerators.                               |
|                                                                   |
| 4.  Simplify if possible.                                         |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Add and subtract mixed numbers                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
+========================================================================================================================================================+=====================================================================================================================================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 4\frac{1}{5}\  + 2\frac{3}{10}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 3\frac{1}{4}\  - 2\frac{1}{3}$$ |
|                                                                                                                                                        |                                                                                                                                                     |
| 1\. Convert to improper $\frac{21}{5}$ $+$ $\ \frac{23}{10}$                                                                                           | 1\. Convert to improper $\frac{13}{4}$ $-$ $\frac{7}{3}$                                                                                            |
|                                                                                                                                                        |                                                                                                                                                     |
| 2\. Same denominators $\frac{42}{10}$ $+$ $\frac{23}{10}$                                                                                              | 2\. Same denominators $\frac{39}{12}$ $-$ $\frac{28}{12}$                                                                                           |
|                                                                                                                                                        |                                                                                                                                                     |
| 3\. Add numerators $\frac{65}{10}$                                                                                                                     | 3\. Subtract numerators $\frac{11}{12}$                                                                                                             |
|                                                                                                                                                        |                                                                                                                                                     |
| 4\. Simplify $\frac{13}{2}$ $= 6$ $\frac{1}{2}$                                                                                                        |                                                                                                                                                     |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                                                                                 |
+=========================================+=======================================+===========================================+=========================================+
| Add and subtract these fractions.                                                                                                                                     |
+-----------------------------------------+---------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------+
| a.                                      | b.                                    | c.                                        | d.                                      |
|                                         |                                       |                                           |                                         |
| $$\ \ \ \ 2\frac{3}{4} + 1\frac{2}{8}$$ | $$\ \ \ 4\frac{1}{5} - 2\frac{3}{4}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ 3\frac{2}{5} - 2\frac{3}{4}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ 1\frac{2}{3} + 6\frac{1}{2}$$ |
|                                         |                                       |                                           |                                         |
| $$= \frac{}{4}\  + \ \ \frac{}{8}$$     | $$= \frac{}{5} - \ \ \frac{}{4}$$     |                                           |                                         |
|                                         |                                       |                                           |                                         |
| $$= \frac{}{8}\  + \ \frac{}{8}$$       | $$= \frac{}{} - \ \frac{}{}$$         |                                           |                                         |
|                                         |                                       |                                           |                                         |
| $$=$$                                   | $$=$$                                 |                                           |                                         |
+-----------------------------------------+---------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Adding and Subtracting Mixed Numbers (Alternate Method)**     |
+===================================================================+
| 1.  Split the mixed numbers to wholes and fractions. Keep the     |
|     sign for subtraction.                                         |
|                                                                   |
| 2.  Sum the wholes and sum the fractions                          |
|                                                                   |
| 3.  Simplify if possible.                                         |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Add and subtract mixed numbers                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
+========================================================================================================================+=======================================================================================================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 4\frac{1}{5}\  + 2\frac{3}{10}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 150\frac{1}{4}\  - 147\frac{1}{3}$$ |
|                                                                                                                        |                                                                                                                       |
| 1\. Split $4 +$ $\frac{1}{5}$ $+ 2 +$ $\frac{3}{10}$                                                                   | 1\. Split $150 +$ $\frac{1}{4}$ $- 147 -$ $\frac{1}{3}$                                                               |
|                                                                                                                        |                                                                                                                       |
| 2\. Sum separately $6 +$ $\frac{2}{10}$ $+$ $\frac{3}{10}$                                                             | 2\. Sum separately $3 +$ $\frac{3}{12}$ $-$ $\frac{4}{12}$                                                            |
|                                                                                                                        |                                                                                                                       |
| $6$ $\frac{5}{10}$                                                                                                     | $3 -$ $\frac{1}{12}$                                                                                                  |
|                                                                                                                        |                                                                                                                       |
| 3\. Simplify $6$ $\frac{1}{2}$                                                                                         | $2$ $\frac{11}{12}$                                                                                                   |
+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                           |
+=================================================+===============================================+
| Add and subtract these fractions                                                                |
+-------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------+
| a.                                              | b.                                            |
|                                                 |                                               |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ 12\frac{1}{4} + 15\frac{3}{7}$$     | $$\ \ \ \ \ 18\frac{2}{3} - 12\frac{1}{5}$$   |
+-------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------+
| c.                                              | d.                                            |
|                                                 |                                               |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ 2250\frac{3}{5} + 700\frac{1}{25}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ 950\frac{1}{2} - 850\frac{2}{9}$$ |
+-------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------+

+=========================================================+=======================================================================================+

|     height="1.532979002624672in"}                       |                                                                                       |
|                                                         | $$1\frac{9}{10}$$                                                                     |
| $$1\frac{7}{20}$$                                       |                                                                                       |

|     height="1.5948862642169728in"}                      |                                                                                       |
|                                                         | $$5\frac{11}{12}$$                                                                    |
| $$2\frac{17}{35}$$                                      |                                                                                       |

2.  Add and subtract these fractions.

+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| a.  $1$              | e.  $2$              | i.  $2$              |
|     $\frac{1}{2}$    |     $\frac{1}{7}$    |     $\frac{1}{2}$    |
|     $+$ $1$          |     $+$ $1$          |     $-$ $2$          |
|     $\frac{1}{3}$    |     $\frac{1}{3}$    |     $\frac{1}{4}$    |
|                      |                      |                      |
| $$2\frac{5}{6}$$     | $$3\frac{10}{21}$$   | $$\frac{1}{4}$$      |
+======================+======================+======================+
| b.  $1$              | f.  $2$              | j.  $2$              |
|     $\frac{1}{2}$    |     $\frac{1}{7}$    |     $\frac{1}{4}$    |
|     $+$ $1$          |     $-$ $1$          |     $-$ $2$          |
|     $\frac{1}{4}$    |     $\frac{1}{3}$    |     $\frac{1}{2}$    |
|                      |                      |                      |
| $$2\frac{3}{4}$$     | $$\frac{17}{21}$$    | $$- \frac{1}{4}$$    |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| c.  $1$              | g.  $2$              | k.  $3$              |
|     $\frac{1}{2}$    |     $\frac{1}{2}$    |     $\frac{1}{5}$    |
|     $+$ $1$          |     $-$ $1$          |     $-$ $2$          |
|     $\frac{1}{5}$    |     $\frac{1}{3}$    |     $\frac{1}{2}$    |
|                      |                      |                      |
| $$2\frac{7}{10}$$    | $$1\frac{1}{6}$$     | $$\frac{7}{10}$$     |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| d.  $2$              | h.  $2$              | l.  $3$              |
|     $\frac{1}{2}$    |     $\frac{1}{2}$    |     $\frac{1}{5}$    |
|     $+$ $1$          |     $-$ $1$          |     $+$ $2$          |
|     $\frac{1}{5}$    |     $\frac{1}{4}$    |     $\frac{1}{2}$    |
|                      |                      |                      |
| $$3\frac{7}{10}$$    | $$1\frac{1}{4}$$     | $$5\frac{7}{10}$$    |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+

3.  

    a.  Work out $1\frac{1}{6} + 3\frac{3}{4}$ by converting each mixed
        number into an improper fraction.

![](media/image76.png){width="5.471135170603675in"
height="0.7538965441819773in"}\
$$1\frac{1}{6} + 3\frac{3}{4}$$

$$= \frac{7}{6} + \frac{15}{4}$$

$$= \frac{14}{12} + \frac{45}{12}$$

$$= \frac{59}{12}$$

$$= 4\frac{11}{12}$$

b.  Work out $1\frac{1}{6} + 3\frac{3}{4}$ by first adding the wholes
    and then adding the fractions.

![](media/image77.png){width="5.448818897637795in"
height="0.7502088801399825in"}\
$$1 + 3 + \frac{1}{6} + \frac{3}{4}$$

$$= 4 + \frac{2}{12} + \frac{9}{12}$$

$$= 4\frac{11}{12}$$

c.  Which method do you prefer?

The second method is a bit easier as you work with smaller numbers.

4.  It is also possible to subtract fractions by subtracting the wholes,
    subtracting the parts.

+---------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------+
| **Worked Example**                          | **Your Turn**                             |
+=============================================+===========================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ 5\frac{2}{10} - 4\frac{3}{10}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ 4\frac{1}{5} - 2\frac{3}{5}$$ |
|                                             |                                           |
| $$= 5 + \frac{2}{10} - 4 - \frac{3}{10}$$   | $$\frac{8}{5}$$                           |
|                                             |                                           |
| $$= 1 + \frac{2}{10} - \frac{3}{10}$$       |                                           |
|                                             |                                           |
| $$= 1 - \frac{1}{10}$$                      |                                           |
|                                             |                                           |
| $$= \frac{9}{10}$$                          |                                           |
+---------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------+

**Development**

5.  Use your preferred method to answer these questions.

+---------------------------------------+------------------------------------+-------------------------------------+
| a.                                    | b.                                 | c.                                  |
|                                       |                                    |                                     |
| > $$2\frac{1}{3} + 2\frac{1}{4}$$     | > $$3\frac{2}{7} + 1\frac{2}{5}$$  | > $$4\frac{7}{9} + 3\frac{2}{3}$$   |
|                                       |                                    |                                     |
| $$4\frac{7}{12}$$                     | $$4\frac{24}{35}$$                 | $$8\frac{4}{9}$$                    |
+=======================================+====================================+=====================================+
| d.                                    | e.                                 | f.                                  |
|                                       |                                    |                                     |
| > $$1\frac{5}{6} - \frac{1}{3}$$      | > $$3\frac{7}{12} - 1\frac{3}{8}$$ | > $$2\frac{4}{5} - 2\frac{7}{9}$$   |
|                                       |                                    |                                     |
| $$1\frac{1}{2}$$                      | $$2\frac{5}{24}$$                  | $$\frac{1}{45}$$                    |
+---------------------------------------+------------------------------------+-------------------------------------+
| g.                                    | h.                                 | i.                                  |
|                                       |                                    |                                     |
| > $$4\frac{1}{5} + 2\frac{3}{10}$$    | > $$3\frac{1}{5} + 1\frac{7}{15}$$ | > $$5\frac{1}{10} + 6\frac{7}{15}$$ |
|                                       |                                    |                                     |
| $$6\frac{1}{2}$$                      | $$4\frac{2}{3}$$                   | $$11\frac{17}{30}$$                 |
+---------------------------------------+------------------------------------+-------------------------------------+
| j.                                    | k.                                 | l.                                  |
|                                       |                                    |                                     |
| > $$12\frac{3}{10} + 23\frac{7}{15}$$ | > $$9\frac{3}{4} + 10\frac{5}{6}$$ | > $$4\frac{2}{3} + 2\frac{3}{5}$$   |
|                                       |                                    |                                     |
| $$35\frac{23}{30}$$                   | $$20\frac{7}{12}$$                 | $$7\frac{4}{15}$$                   |

Mastery

8.  Rectangles A and B have the same perimeter. Find the missing length.

![](media/image83.png){width="3.3333333333333335in"
height="2.4590277777777776in"}

$$P_{A} = 2\left( 2\frac{3}{4} + 4\frac{1}{6} \right) = 13\frac{5}{6}$$

$$P_{B} = 2x + 2\left( 6\frac{2}{3} \right) = 2x + 13\frac{1}{3}$$

$$2x = \frac{1}{2}\ cm$$

$$x = \frac{1}{4}\ cm$$
