# Multiplying and Dividing by Rational Numbers

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Multiplying by Rational Numbers**                             |
+===================================================================+
| When you **multiply** a number by:                                |
|                                                                   |
| - A number **less than 1**, your **answer is smaller** than your  |
|   starting number.                                                |
|                                                                   |
| - The number 1, your answer equals your starting number.          |
|                                                                   |
| - A number **greater than 1**, your **answer is larger** than     |
|   your starting number.                                           |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Identify** the effect of multiplying by a rational number                                             |
+=================+=================+=================+=================+=================+=================+
| $$\times 3$$    | $$\times 0.3$$                    | $$\times \frac{1}{3}$$            | $$\times 3.3$$  |
|                 |                                   |                                   |                 |
| Result is       | Result is smaller                 | Result is smaller                 | Result is       |
| larger          |                                   |                                   | larger          |
+-----------------+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+-----------------+
| Decide whether the results of these multiplications will be larger or smaller than the original           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| a.                                | b.                                | c.                                |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| $$\times 10$$                     | $$\times \frac{1}{10}$$           | $$\times \frac{11}{10}$$          |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| Result is:                        | Result is:                        | Result is:                        |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Smaller                         | - Smaller                         | - Smaller                         |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Larger                          | - Larger                          | - Larger                          |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Same                            | - Same                            | - Same                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| d.                                | e.                                | f.                                |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| $$\times \frac{10}{10}$$          | $$\times 0.10$$                   | $$\times 1.11$$                   |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| Result is:                        | Result is:                        | Result is:                        |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Smaller                         | - Smaller                         | - Smaller                         |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Larger                          | - Larger                          | - Larger                          |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Same                            | - Same                            | - Same                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Dividing by Rational Numbers**                                |
+===================================================================+
| When you **divide** a number by:                                  |
|                                                                   |
| - A number **less than 1**, your **answer is larger** than your   |
|   starting number.                                                |
|                                                                   |
| - The number 1, your answer equals your starting number.          |
|                                                                   |
| - A number **greater than 1**, your **answer is smaller** than    |
|   your starting number.                                           |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Identify** the effect of dividing by a rational number                                                |
+=================+=================+=================+=================+=================+=================+
| $$\div 3$$      | $$\div 0.3$$                      | $$\div \frac{1}{3}$$              | $$\div 3.3$$    |
|                 |                                   |                                   |                 |
| Result is       | Result is larger                  | Result is larger                  | Result is       |
| smaller         |                                   |                                   | smaller         |
+-----------------+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+-----------------+
| Decide whether the results of these divisions will be larger or smaller than the original                 |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| a.                                | b.                                | c.                                |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| $$\div 7$$                        | $$\div \frac{1}{7}$$              | $$\div \frac{6}{7}$$              |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| Result is:                        | Result is:                        | Result is:                        |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Smaller                         | - Smaller                         | - Smaller                         |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Larger                          | - Larger                          | - Larger                          |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Same                            | - Same                            | - Same                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| d.                                | e.                                | f.                                |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| $$\div \frac{8}{7}$$              | $$\div 0.87$$                     | $$\div \frac{8}{8}$$              |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| Result is:                        | Result is:                        | Result is:                        |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Smaller                         | - Smaller                         | - Smaller                         |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Larger                          | - Larger                          | - Larger                          |
|                                   |                                   |                                   |
| - Same                            | - Same                            | - Same                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Foundation

1.  Using a calculator, or mentally, complete the table.

+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| **Original | **Multiplier**           | **Product** | **Smaller, equal,  |
| number**   |                          |             | or larger compared |
|            |                          |             | to original?**     |
+===========:+==========================+=============+:==================:+
| 12         | $$\times 0.5$$           | = 6         | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | smaller            |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 7          | $$\times 1$$             | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | equal              |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 15         | $$\times 1.5$$           | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| $$20$$     | $$\times 0.2$$           | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | smaller            |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 10         | $$\times 2.5$$           | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 5          | $$\times 0.2$$           | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | smaller            |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 40         | $$\times 0.9$$           | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | smaller            |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 6          | $$\times 1.1$$           | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 12         | $$\times \frac{1}{3}$$   | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | smaller            |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 20         | $$\times \frac{3}{4}$$   | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | smaller            |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 40         | $$\times \frac{8}{8}$$   | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | equal              |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 6          | $$\times \frac{5}{4}$$   | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 15         | $$\times \frac{11}{5}$$  | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+
| 16         | $$\times \frac{13}{13}$$ | =           | smaller equal      |
|            |                          |             | larger             |
|            |                          |             |                    |
|            |                          |             | equal              |
+------------+--------------------------+-------------+--------------------+

2.  Complete these sentences:

> Word bank (reusing allowed): less, greater, smaller, equal, proper,
> improper, one
>
> When we multiply numbers, the result depends on the multiplier
> involved.
>
> If we multiply a number by a number that is ..................... than
> 1, such as a .................. fraction like $\frac{3}{4}$ or a
> decimal like 0.8, the product will always be .....................
> than the original number.

smaller, proper, smaller

> If we multiply a number by a factor ..................... than 1, such
> as an ..................... fraction like $\frac{5}{4}$ or a whole
> number greater than 1, the product will always be
> ..................... than the original number.

greater, improper, greater

> When we multiply a number by exactly ..................... the product
> is ..................... to the original number. This is true whether
> we express 1 as a whole number, a fraction like $\frac{5}{5}$, or a
> decimal like 1.00.

one, equal

5.  Complete these sentences:

> Word bank: less, greater, smaller, equal, proper, improper, one,
> opposite

When we divide numbers, the result depends on the divisor involved.

> If we divide a number by a number that is .................. than 1,
> such as a .................. fraction like $\frac{3}{4}$ or a decimal
> like 0.8, the quotient will always be .................. than the
> original number.

Smaller, proper, greater

> If we divide a number by a number .................. than 1, such as
> an .................. fraction like\
> $\frac{5}{4}$ or a whole number greater than 1, the quotient will
> always be .................. than the original number.

Greater, improper, smaller

> When we divide a number by exactly .................. the quotient is
> .................. to the original number. This is true whether we
> express 1 as a whole number, a fraction like $\frac{5}{5}$, or a
> decimal like 1.00.

one, equal

> It\'s important to note that these rules for division are the
> .................. of those for multiplication. While multiplication
> by a number less than 1 makes the result smaller, division by a number
> less than 1 makes the result larger.

opposite

    larger than the original.

# Multiplying Fractions and Integers

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Multiplying Fractions and Integers**                          |
+===================================================================+
| When multiplying a fraction and a whole number, we can think of   |
| it as repeated addition.                                          |
|                                                                   |
| $$\frac{a}{b} \times c = \frac{a \times c}{b}$$                   |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Multiply fractions using visual models                                                                  |
+===================================================================================+===================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{2}{5} \times 3$$                                                | Why does the denominator not      |
|                                                                                   | change when multiplying fractions |
| ![](media/image87.png){width="1.0138888888888888in"                               | by whole numbers?                 |
| height="0.42986111111111114in"}![](media/image88.png){width="2.441666666666667in" |                                   |
| height="0.4409722222222222in"}\                                                   | *Multiplying by a whole number    |
| $$= \frac{6}{5}$$                                                                 | means repeated                    |
|                                                                                   | ..................; when we       |
|                                                                                   | ......... fractions, we do not    |
|                                                                                   | change the denominator.*          |
+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ 6 \times \frac{2}{3}$$                                                | Why does the order not matter     |
|                                                                                   | when multiplying integers and     |
| ![](media/image89.png){width="1.2194444444444446in"                               | fractions?                        |
| height="0.7138888888888889in"}![](media/image90.png){width="1.84375in"            |                                   |
| height="0.6875in"}                                                                | *We can ............... numbers   |
|                                                                                   | in any order and the answer is    |
| $$= \frac{12}{3}$$                                                                | the same.*                        |
|                                                                                   |                                   |
| $= 4$                                                                             |                                   |
+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                                                                                      |
+========================================================================================+===================================================================================+

Foundation

1.  Multiply these fractions using the diagrams.

+----------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------------------+
| a.  ![](media/image98.png){width="1.9868055555555555in"  | b.  ![](media/image99.png){width="1.6403510498687663in"  |
|     height="0.6402777777777777in"}                       |     height="0.592173009623797in"}                        |
|                                                          |                                                          |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{6} \times 4$$                       | $$\ \ \ \ \ 3 \times \frac{3}{4}$$                       |
|                                                          |                                                          |
| ![](media/image98.png){width="0.5284722222222222in"      | ![](media/image100.png){width="1.640528215223097in"      |
| height="0.6402777777777777in"}                           | height="0.5618842957130359in"}                           |
|                                                          |                                                          |
| $$= \frac{}{6}$$                                         | $$=$$                                                    |
|                                                          |                                                          |
| $$\frac{4}{6} = \frac{2}{3}$$                            | $$\frac{9}{4} = 2\frac{1}{4}$$                           |
+==========================================================+==========================================================+
| c.  ![](media/image101.png){width="1.1178729221347332in" | d.  ![](media/image102.png){width="1.6902777777777778in" |
|     height="0.7743186789151356in"}                       |     height="1.1090277777777777in"}                       |
|                                                          |                                                          |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{5}{6} \times 2$$                       | $$\ \ \ \ \ 6 \times \frac{3}{8}$$                       |
|                                                          |                                                          |
| ![](media/image101.png){width="1.1178729221347332in"     | ![](media/image102.png){width="1.6881430446194226in"     |
| height="0.7743186789151356in"}                           | height="0.5652055993000875in"}                           |
|                                                          |                                                          |
| $$=$$                                                    | $$=$$                                                    |
|                                                          |                                                          |
| $$\frac{10}{6} = \frac{5}{3}$$                           | $$\frac{18}{8} = \frac{9}{4} = 2\frac{1}{4}$$            |

Which method was easiest for $10 \times$ $\frac{4}{5}$?

Divide, then multiply

Which method was easiest for $6 \times$ $\frac{4}{5}$?

Multiply, then divide

How might you decide whether to multiply first or divide first?

Divide first if the quotient will be a whole number.

Solve these problems, choosing whether to divide or multiply first.

+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| a.  40 $\times$      | b.  18 $\times$      | c.  5 $\times$       |

|                      |                      |                      |
| $$18$$               | $$70$$               | $$\frac{75}{4}$$     |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+

10. Calculate these answers by splitting the mixed numeral, then using
    the distributive law.

+-----------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------+
| a.  $8 \times 5\frac{1}{2} = 8 \times \left( 5 + \frac{1}{2} \right)$ | b.  $20 \times 3\frac{1}{4}$    |
|                                                                       |                                 |
| $=$ $(8 \times 5) + \left( 8 \times \frac{1}{2} \right)$              | 65                              |
|                                                                       |                                 |
| $=$ ..................                                                |                                 |
|                                                                       |                                 |
| 44                                                                    |                                 |
+=======================================================================+=================================+

|                                                                       |                                 |
| 28                                                                    | 66                              |

# Multiplying Fractions using Models

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Multiplication of Fractions**                                                                           |
+=======================================================+=====================================================+
| We can think of multiplication in two ways:                                                                 |
+-------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------+
| $$2 \times \frac{1}{3} = \frac{2}{3}$$                | $$\frac{1}{3} \times \frac{1}{2} = \frac{1}{6}$$    |
|                                                       |                                                     |
| ![Right click to save                                 | ![](media/image109.png){width="0.813432852143482in" |
| me!](media/image108.png){width="0.7868055555555555in" | height="0.8408934820647419in"}"what is one-third of |
| height="0.7868055555555555in"}![Right click to save   | one-half?"                                          |
| me!](media/image108.png){width="0.7868055555555555in" |                                                     |
| height="0.7868055555555555in"}"what is two lots of    |                                                     |
| one third?"                                           |                                                     |
+-------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------+
| - Fraction Multiplication: <https://www.geogebra.org/m/f526fmeh>                                            |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Multiply fractions using visual models                                                                            |
+============================================+====================================================================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \frac{1}{2} \times \frac{1}{3}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \frac{2}{3} \times \frac{3}{5}$$                                         |
|                                            |                                                                                    |
| $$= \frac{1}{6}$$                          | ![](media/image110.png){width="1.3743055555555554in"                               |
|                                            | height="1.5763888888888888in"}![](media/image111.png){width="1.3847222222222222in" |
|                                            | height="1.542361111111111in"}                                                      |
|                                            |                                                                                    |
|                                            | $$= \frac{6}{15}$$                                                                 |
+--------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                                                 |
+========================================================================================+==============================================+
| a.  ![](media/image112.png){width="1.4666666666666666in"                               | b.  ![](media/image113.png){width="1.4625in" |
|     height="1.6381944444444445in"}                                                     |     height="1.695138888888889in"}            |
|                                                                                        |                                              |
| $$\ \ \ \ \frac{1}{2} \times \frac{1}{7}$$                                             | $$\ \ \ \ \frac{5}{7} \times \frac{1}{2}$$   |
|                                                                                        |                                              |
| $$= \frac{}{}$$                                                                        | $$= \frac{}{}$$                              |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+

# Multiplying Fractions using the Rule

+--------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Multiplying Fractions**                                        |
+====================================================================+
| Multiply the numerators and multiply the denominators              |
|                                                                    |
| The word 'of' means to multiply.                                   |
|                                                                    |
| $$\frac{a}{b} \times \frac{c}{d} = \frac{a \times c}{b \times d}$$ |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Multiply fractions using the rule                                             |
+==============================================+==============================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{2} \times \frac{1}{3}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{2}{3} \times \frac{3}{5}$$ |
|                                              |                                              |
| $$= \frac{1 \times 1}{2 \times 3}$$          | $$= \frac{2 \times 3}{3 \times 5}$$          |
|                                              |                                              |
| $$= \frac{1}{6}$$                            | $$= \frac{6}{15} = \frac{2}{5}$$             |
+----------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------+

+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                                             |
+=================================================================+=================================================================+
| a.                                                              | b.                                                              |
|                                                                 |                                                                 |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{1}{5} \times \frac{3}{4}$$                    | $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{2}{3} \times \frac{3}{4}$$                    |
|                                                                 |                                                                 |
| $$= \frac{\ \ \  \times \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \  \times \ \ \ \ \ }$$ | $$= \frac{\ \ \  \times \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \  \times \ \ \ \ \ }$$ |
|                                                                 |                                                                 |
| $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ }$$                             | $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ }$$                       |
+-----------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+
| c.                                                              | d.                                                              |
|                                                                 |                                                                 |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \frac{2}{5} \times 3$$                              | $$\ \ \ \ \frac{5}{2} \times \frac{3}{4}$$                      |
+-----------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+
| e.                                                              | f.                                                              |
|                                                                 |                                                                 |
| $\frac{1}{3}$ of 12                                             | $\frac{3}{4}$ of $\frac{1}{5}$                                  |
+-----------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------+

    over 1.

| a.                                                          | b.                          | c.                          |

| >                                                           |                             |                             |
| > $=$                                                       | $$16$$                      | $$15$$                      |
|                                                             |                             |                             |
| $$\frac{5}{2}$$                                             |                             |                             |
+=============================================================+=============================+=============================+
| d.                                                          | e.                          | f.                          |
|                                                             |                             |                             |
| > $$\frac{2}{7}\ of\ 42$$                                   | > $$\frac{1}{4}\ of\ 16$$   | > $$\frac{1}{5}\ of\ 45$$   |
|                                                             |                             |                             |
| 12                                                          | 4                           | 9                           |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------+-----------------------------+

Explain why the rule "multiply by the numerator and keep the denominator
the same"\
works when multiplying a whole number and a fraction.

When multiplying by a whole number, you can think of it as repeated
addition. When you add fractions, the denominator doesn't change.

9.  **\[JMO 1996 A4\]** Evaluate

$$\left\lbrack \left( \frac{1}{2} + \frac{1}{3} \right) + \frac{1}{4} \right\rbrack \times \frac{1}{5} - \frac{1}{6}$$

> $$\left\lbrack \left( \frac{3}{6} + \frac{2}{6} \right) + \frac{1}{4} \right\rbrack \times \frac{1}{5} - \frac{1}{6}$$
>
> $$= \left( \frac{5}{6} + \frac{1}{4} \right) \times \frac{1}{5} - \frac{1}{6}$$
>
> $$= \left( \frac{20}{24} + \frac{6}{24} \right) \times \frac{1}{5} - \frac{1}{6}$$
>
> $$= \frac{26}{24} \times \frac{1}{5} - \frac{1}{6}$$
>
> $$= \frac{13}{12} \times \frac{1}{5} - \frac{1}{6}$$
>
> $$= \frac{13}{60} - \frac{1}{6}$$
>
> $$= \frac{13}{60} - \frac{10}{60}$$
>
> $$= \frac{3}{60}$$
>
> $$= \frac{1}{20}$$

10. To find half of a fraction, you can either halve the numerator or
    double the denominator:

+------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------+
| Half of $\frac{4}{5} = \frac{2}{5}$ (halve the | Half of $\frac{7}{10} = \frac{3.5}{10}$ (halve   |
| numerator)                                     | the numerator)                                   |
|                                                |                                                  |
|                                                | $= \frac{7}{20}$ (simplify)                      |
+================================================+==================================================+
| Half of                                        | Half of                                          |
| $\frac{4}{5} = \frac{1}{2} \times \frac{4}{5}$ | $\frac{7}{10} = \frac{1}{2} \times \frac{7}{10}$ |
|                                                |                                                  |
| $= \frac{4}{10}$ (double the denominator)      | $= \frac{7}{20}$ (double the denominator)        |
|                                                |                                                  |
| $= \frac{2}{5}$ (simplify)                     |                                                  |
+------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------+

Find half of these fractions by either halving the denominator or
multiplying by $\frac{1}{2}$

+---------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| a.  Half of $\frac{8}{9}$       | b.  Half of $\frac{5}{9}$        |
|                                 |                                  |
| Halve the numerator:            | Halve the numerator:             |
|                                 |                                  |
| $$\frac{4}{9}$$                 | $$\frac{2.5}{9} = \frac{5}{18}$$ |
|                                 |                                  |
| Double the denominator:         | Double the denominator:          |
|                                 |                                  |
| $$\frac{8}{18} = \frac{4}{9}$$  | $$\frac{5}{18}$$                 |
+=================================+==================================+

> When might it be easier to halve the numerator and when might it be
> easier to double the denominator?

Halve the numerator if the quotient will be a whole number.

Calculate the following using the easier method:

+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| a.  Half of          | b.  Half of          | c.  Half of          |
|     $\frac{3}{4}$    |     $\frac{20}{21}$  |     $8\frac{9}{11}$  |
|                      |                      |                      |
| $$\frac{3}{8}$$      | $$\frac{10}{21}$$    | $$4\frac{9}{22}$$    |
+======================+======================+======================+
| d.  A third of       | e.  A third of       | f.  A quarter of     |
|     $\frac{3}{4}$    |     $\frac{7}{10}$   |     $\frac{1}{5}$    |
|                      |                      |                      |
| $$\frac{1}{4}$$      | $$\frac{7}{30}$$     | $$\frac{1}{20}$$     |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| g.  A quarter of     | h.  A fifth of       | i.  A fifth of       |
|     $\frac{12}{13}$  |     $\frac{15}{16}$  |     $20\frac{1}{3}$  |
|                      |                      |                      |
| $$\frac{3}{13}$$     | $$\frac{3}{16}$$     | $$4\frac{1}{15}$$    |

# Multiplying Mixed Numerals

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Multiplying Mixed Numerals**                                  |
+===================================================================+
| 1.  Convert mixed numbers to improper fractions: $a$              |
|     $\frac{b}{n} = \frac{a \times n + b}{n}$                      |
|                                                                   |
| 2.  Multiply the numerators and multiply the denominators.        |
|                                                                   |
| 3.  Simplify if possible.                                         |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Multiply mixed numbers using the rule                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
+============================================================================================================================================+============================================================================================================================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 1\frac{3}{5} \times 2\frac{1}{3}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2\frac{2}{3} \times 3\frac{1}{2}$$ |
|                                                                                                                                            |                                                                                                                                            |
| 1\. Convert to improper $\frac{8}{5}$ $\times$ $\frac{7}{3}$                                                                               | 1\. Convert to improper $\frac{8}{3}$ $\times$ $\frac{7}{2}$                                                                               |
|                                                                                                                                            |                                                                                                                                            |
| 2\. Multiply $\frac{56}{15}$                                                                                                               | 2\. Multiply $\frac{56}{6}$                                                                                                                |
|                                                                                                                                            |                                                                                                                                            |
|                                                                                                                                            | 3\. Simplify $\frac{28}{3}$                                                                                                                |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                               |
+================================================+====================================================================+
| e.                                             | f.                                                                 |
|                                                |                                                                    |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ 1\frac{1}{5} \times 2\frac{3}{4}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ 2\frac{2}{5} \times 1\frac{1}{6}$$                     |
|                                                |                                                                    |
| $$= \ \frac{6}{5}\ \  \times \ \frac{11}{4}$$  | $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{5}\ \  \times \ \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ }{6}$$ |
|                                                |                                                                    |
| $$= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ }$$          |                                                                    |
|                                                |                                                                    |
| $= \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ }$l           |                                                                    |
+------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------+
| g.                                             | h.                                                                 |
|                                                |                                                                    |
| $$\ \ \ \ \ 2 \times 3\frac{2}{7}$$            | $$\ \ \ \ \ 2\frac{1}{5} \times 4\frac{3}{4}$$                     |
+------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Key Ideas**                                                   |
+===================================================================+
| 3.  It is most efficient to convert any mixed numbers to          |
|     .................. .................. before multiplying.     |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

Foundation

1.  Multiply these fractions.

+------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------+
| a.                                                   | b.  ![](media/image127.png){width="1.0291666666666666in"                               | c.                                   |
|                                                      |     height="1.8340277777777778in"}![](media/image128.png){width="1.4659722222222222in" |                                      |
| $$4\frac{2}{3} \times \frac{5}{6}$$                  |     height="1.9284722222222221in"}![](media/image127.png){width="1.0294116360454943in" | $$4\frac{3}{4} \times \frac{2}{5}$$  |
|                                                      |     height="1.834417104111986in"}                                                      |                                      |
| $$3\frac{8}{9}$$                                     |                                                                                        | $$1\frac{9}{10}$$                    |
|                                                      | $$\frac{2}{3} \times 2\frac{1}{2}$$                                                    |                                      |
|                                                      |                                                                                        |                                      |
|                                                      | $$1\frac{2}{3}$$                                                                       |                                      |
+======================================================+========================================================================================+======================================+
| d.                                                   | e.  ![](media/image127.png){width="1.0291666666666666in"                               | f.                                   |
|                                                      |     height="1.8340277777777778in"}![](media/image127.png){width="1.0294116360454943in" |                                      |
| $$\frac{5}{12} \times 2\frac{3}{5}$$                 |     height="1.834417104111986in"}                                                      | $$2\frac{3}{4} \times 1\frac{3}{5}$$ |
|                                                      |                                                                                        |                                      |
| ![](media/image127.png){width="1.0291666666666666in" | $$6\frac{1}{2} \times \frac{2}{7}$$                                                    | $$4\frac{2}{5}$$                     |
| height="1.8340277777777778in"}                       |                                                                                        |                                      |
|                                                      | $$1\frac{6}{7}$$                                                                       |                                      |
| $$1\frac{1}{12}$$                                    |                                                                                        |                                      |
+------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------+
| g.                                                   | h.                                                                                     | i.                                   |
|                                                      |                                                                                        |                                      |
| $$5\frac{1}{3} \times 1\frac{1}{2}$$                 | $$1\frac{2}{3} \times 2\frac{1}{4}$$                                                   | $$2\frac{2}{5} \times 1\frac{1}{2}$$ |
|                                                      |                                                                                        |                                      |
| $$8$$                                                | $$3\frac{3}{4}$$                                                                       | $$3\frac{3}{5}$$                     |
+------------------------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+--------------------------------------+

2.  To paint one classroom, 2 $\frac{1}{3}$ litres of paint are
    required.\
    How many litres of paint are required to paint five identical
    classrooms?

$$11\frac{2}{3}\ litres$$

3.  A scone recipe requires 1 $\frac{3}{4}$ cups of flour and
    $\frac{3}{4}$ of a cup of cream.\
    Jamie is catering for a large group and needs to quadruple the
    recipe.\
    How much flour and how much cream will she need?

7 cups flour and 3 cups cream

Development

4.  It takes $2\frac{1}{4}$ hours to paint a fence. One quarter of this
    time is spent sanding the wood down. What fraction of an hour is
    spent in sanding the wood?

$$\frac{9}{16}\ hours$$

5.  $\frac{3}{5}$ of a road is to be resurfaced.\
    If the road is $1\frac{1}{2}$ km long, what length in kilometres is
    to be resurfaced?

$$\frac{9}{10}$$

6.  If you spent $1\frac{1}{2}$ hours on homework last night and
    $\frac{1}{4}$ of that time was on history,\
    how long did you spend on history?

$$\frac{3}{8}$$

7.  Read the example carefully and answer the questions.

# Simplify Before You Multiply

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Simplifying Fractions Before You Multiply**                   |
+===================================================================+
| - Fraction multiplication is easier if you simplify or "cancel"   |
|   the fractions before multiplying.                               |
|                                                                   |
| - Simplifying means to divide the numerator and denominator by a  |
|   common factor.                                                  |
|                                                                   |
| ![Diagram Description automatically generated with low            |
| confidence](media/image132.png){width="5.1305555555555555in"      |
| height="1.4513888888888888in"}                                    |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Simplify fraction before multiplying                                                                                                                                                               |
+========================================================================================================+=========================================================================================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{4}{8}\  \times \ \frac{3}{2}$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \frac{2}{3}\  \times \ \frac{12}{5}$$ |
|                                                                                                        |                                                                                                         |
| 1\. Simplify $\frac{1}{2}$ $\times$ $\frac{3}{2}$                                                      | 1\. Simplify $\frac{2}{1}$ $\times$ $\frac{4}{5}$                                                       |
|                                                                                                        |                                                                                                         |
| 2\. Multiply $\frac{3}{4}$                                                                             | 2\. Multiply $\frac{8}{5}$                                                                              |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                                                     |
+=====================================================================+=====================================================================+
| Simplify these fractions before multiplying them.                                                                                         |
+---------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------+
| a.  $\frac{7}{3} \times \frac{2}{6}$                                | b.  $\frac{3}{4} \times \frac{4}{7}$                                |
|                                                                     |                                                                     |
| $$\ \ \ \ \  = \frac{7}{3} \times \frac{\ \ \ \ \ \ }{\ \ \ \ \ }$$ | $$\ \ \ \ \ \  = \frac{3}{\ \ \ \ \ } \times \frac{\ \ \ \ \ }{7}$$ |
+---------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------+
| c.  $\frac{5}{9} \times \frac{7}{10}$                               | d.  $\frac{8}{11} \times \frac{3}{4}$                               |
+---------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Key Ideas**                                                   |
+===================================================================+
| 1.  It is most efficient to simplify fractions before you         |
|     ..................... so you work with smaller numbers.       |
|                                                                   |
| 2.  You can simplify ........................ or                  |
|     ........................, but not ........................... |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

Foundation

1.  Multiply by simplifying the highlighted values first.

+------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------+
| a.                                       | b.                                       | c.                                       | d.                                       |
|                                          |                                          |                                          |                                          |
| > $$\frac{5}{7} \times \frac{13}{15} =$$ | > $$\frac{3}{8} \times \frac{11}{12} =$$ | > $$\frac{12}{18} \times \frac{5}{7} =$$ | > $$\frac{4}{16} \times \frac{2}{3} =$$  |
|                                          |                                          |                                          |                                          |
| $$\frac{13}{21}$$                        | $$\frac{11}{32}$$                        | $$\frac{10}{21}$$                        | $$\frac{1}{6}$$                          |
+==========================================+==========================================+==========================================+==========================================+

|                                          |                                          |                                          |                                          |
| > $$\frac{3}{4} \times \frac{12}{48} =$$ | > $$\frac{2}{5} \times \frac{15}{24} =$$ | > $$\frac{8}{12} \times \frac{4}{64} =$$ | > $$\frac{6}{56} \times \frac{7}{12} =$$ |
|                                          |                                          |                                          |                                          |
| $$\frac{3}{16}$$                         | $$\frac{1}{4}$$                          | $$\frac{1}{24}$$                         | $$\frac{1}{16}$$                         |

| a.  $\frac{3}{7}$ of 42                            | b.  $\frac{1}{4}$  | c.  $\frac{4}{5}$ | d.  $\frac{3}{7}$   |

+====================================================+====================+===================+=====================+

|                                                    |     of             |     of            |     of              |
| $$\frac{2}{7}$$                                    |     $\frac{3}{12}$ |     $\frac{2}{5}$ |     $\frac{10}{11}$ |
|                                                    |                    |                   |                     |
|                                                    | $$\frac{1}{6}$$    | $$\frac{3}{10}$$  | $$\frac{4}{11}$$    |
+----------------------------------------------------+--------------------+-------------------+---------------------+

+----------------------------------------+------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------+
| a.                                     | e.                                       | i.                                      |
|                                        |                                          |                                         |
| > $$\frac{2}{9} \times \frac{3}{4}$$   | > $$\frac{4}{27} \times \frac{9}{16}$$   | > $$\frac{27}{8} \times \frac{16}{15}$$ |
|                                        |                                          |                                         |
| $$\frac{1}{6}$$                        | $$\frac{1}{12}$$                         | $$\frac{18}{5}$$                        |
+========================================+==========================================+=========================================+
| b.                                     | f.                                       | j.                                      |
|                                        |                                          |                                         |
| > $$\frac{2}{9} \times \frac{3}{8}$$   | > $$\frac{8}{27} \times \frac{9}{16}$$   | > $$3\frac{3}{8} \times \frac{16}{15}$$ |
|                                        |                                          |                                         |
| $$\frac{1}{12}$$                       | $$\frac{1}{6}$$                          | $$\frac{18}{5}$$                        |
+----------------------------------------+------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------+
| c.                                     | g.                                       | k.                                      |
|                                        |                                          |                                         |
| > $$\frac{4}{9} \times \frac{3}{16}$$  | > $$\frac{8}{27} \times \frac{15}{16}$$  | > $$3\frac{3}{8} \times 1\frac{1}{15}$$ |
|                                        |                                          |                                         |
| $$\frac{1}{12}$$                       | $$\frac{5}{18}$$                         | $$\frac{18}{5}$$                        |
+----------------------------------------+------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------+
| d.                                     | h.                                       | l.                                      |
|                                        |                                          |                                         |
| > $$\frac{4}{27} \times \frac{3}{16}$$ | > $$\frac{16}{27} \times \frac{15}{16}$$ | > $$3\frac{3}{8} \times 1\frac{2}{30}$$ |
|                                        |                                          |                                         |
| $$\frac{1}{36}$$                       | $$\frac{5}{9}$$                          | $$\frac{36}{10}$$                       |
+----------------------------------------+------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------------+

Mastery

6.  Multiply these fractions. It is a good idea to simplify first.\
    Your final answer should be fully simplified.

+----------------------------------------+----------------------------------------+----------------------------------------------------------+
| a.                                     | b.                                     | c.                                                       |
|                                        |                                        |                                                          |
| $$\frac{12}{16} \times \frac{15}{20}$$ | $$\frac{15}{12} \times \frac{24}{45}$$ | $$\frac{6}{8} \times \frac{17}{5} \times \frac{10}{17}$$ |
|                                        |                                        |                                                          |
| $$\frac{9}{16}$$                       | $$\frac{2}{3}$$                        | $$\frac{3}{2}$$                                          |
+========================================+========================================+==========================================================+

7.  Find the value of:

$$2 \times \frac{25}{9} \times \frac{16}{26} \times \frac{18}{8} \times \frac{13}{50} \times \frac{1}{2}$$

$$1$$

8.  Simplify:

$$\frac{1}{2} \times \frac{2}{3} \times \frac{3}{4} \times \ldots\frac{n - 1}{n}$$

$$\frac{1}{n}$$

9.  **\[JMC 2004 Q15\]** Granny spends one third of her weekly pension
    on Thursday night,\
    and one quarter of what remains on Friday.\
    What fraction of the original amount is left for her big night out
    on Saturday?

$$\frac{2}{3} \times \frac{3}{4} = \frac{1}{2}$$

She has half remaining.

10. **\[JMO 2014 A10\]** My four pet monkeys and I harvested a large
    pile of peanuts.\
    Monkey A woke in the night and ate half of them;\
    then Monkey B woke and ate one third of what remained;\
    then Monkey C woke and ate one quarter of the rest;\
    finally Monkey D ate one fifth of the much diminished remaining
    pile.\
    What fraction of the original harvest was left in the morning?

$$\frac{1}{2} \times \frac{2}{3} \times \frac{3}{4} \times \frac{4}{5} = \frac{1}{5}$$

One fifth remains

# Dividing Fractions using Visual Models

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Division of Fractions**                                                               |
+=======================================================+===================================+
| We can think of division in two ways:                                                     |
+-------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| **Quotition division\**                               | **Partition division\**           |
| (divisor less than original)                          | (divisor greater than original)   |
|                                                       |                                   |
| how many parts are there?                             | what is the size of each part?    |
|                                                       |                                   |
| $3 \div$ $\frac{1}{2}$ $= 6$                          | $\frac{1}{2}$ $\div 3 =$          |
|                                                       | $\frac{1}{6}$                     |
| "how many halves are in three wholes?"                |                                   |
|                                                       | "If I divide half into three      |
| ![Right click to save                                 | pieces,\                          |
| me!](media/image140.png){width="0.7874015748031497in" | what is the size of each part?"   |
| height="0.7874015748031497in"}                        |                                   |
|                                                       | ![](media/image144.png)           |
| ![Right click to save                                 |                                   |
| me!](media/image140.png){width="0.7868055555555555in" |                                   |
| height="0.7868055555555555in"}![Right click to save   |                                   |
| me!](media/image140.png){width="0.7868055555555555in" |                                   |
| height="0.7868055555555555in"}                        |                                   |
+-------------------------------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Example** Divide fractions using quotation division                                                     |
+======================================================+======================================================+
| $$\ \ \ \ \ 1 \div \frac{1}{2}\ $$                   | $$\ \ \ \ \ \ 2 \div \frac{2}{3}$$                   |
|                                                      |                                                      |
| ![](media/image142.png){width="1.0555555555555556in" | ![](media/image143.png){width="2.0972222222222223in" |
| height="1.163888888888889in"}                        | height="1.3291666666666666in"}                       |
|                                                      |                                                      |
| $$= 2$$                                              | $$= 3$$                                              |
+------------------------------------------------------+------------------------------------------------------+

+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Guided Practice**                                                                                                                                                           |
+========================================================================================+========================================================================================+

4

3

$$2\frac{2}{3}$$

$$2\frac{1}{2}$$

$$2\frac{1}{4}$$

# Reciprocals

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Reciprocals**                                                 |
+===================================================================+
| Two numbers are **reciprocals** of each other if they multiply to |
| 1.                                                                |
|                                                                   |
| You can think of the reciprocal as **swapping** the **numerator** |
| and **denominator**.                                              |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Identify** reciprocal of a number                                               |
+=====================+===================+=====================+=====================+
| $$\frac{1}{8} \times 8 = 1$$            | $$\frac{2}{3} \times \frac{3}{2} = 1$$    |
|                                         |                                           |
| The reciprocal of $\frac{1}{8}$ is 8.   | The reciprocal of $\frac{2}{3}$ is        |
|                                         | $\frac{3}{2}$.                            |
| The reciprocal of 8 is $\frac{1}{8}$    |                                           |
|                                         | The reciprocal of $\frac{3}{2}$ is        |
|                                         | $\frac{2}{3}$                             |
+-----------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------+
| Identify the reciprocal of these numbers.                                           |
+---------------------+-----------------------------------------+---------------------+
| a.                  | b.                                      | c.                  |
|                     |                                         |                     |
| $$5$$               | $$3$$                                   | $$113$$             |
+---------------------+-----------------------------------------+---------------------+
| d.                  | e.                                      | f.                  |
|                     |                                         |                     |
| $$1$$               | $$\frac{1}{5}$$                         | $$\frac{1}{7}$$     |
+---------------------+-----------------------------------------+---------------------+
| g.                  | h.                                      | i.                  |
|                     |                                         |                     |
| $$\frac{1}{2754}$$  | $$\frac{3}{1}$$                         | $$\frac{3}{3}$$     |
+---------------------+-----------------------------------------+---------------------+
| j.                  | k.                                      | l.                  |
|                     |                                         |                     |
| $$1\frac{1}{3}$$    | $$2\frac{3}{5}$$                        | $$0.5$$             |
+---------------------+-----------------------------------------+---------------------+
| m.                  | n.                                      | o.                  |
|                     |                                         |                     |
| $$n$$               | $$\frac{1}{n}$$                         | $$\frac{a}{b}$$     |
+---------------------+-----------------------------------------+---------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
| - **Key Ideas**                                                   |
+===================================================================+
| 1.  The product of a number and its .................. is 1.      |
|                                                                   |
| 2.  An easy way to determine the reciprocal of a fraction is to   |
|     ............ the numerator and denominator.                   |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Foundation**

1.  Write the reciprocals of these fractions.

+------------------------------+------------------------------+------------------------------+------------------------------+
| a.                           | b.                           | c.                           | d.                           |
|                              |                              |                              |                              |
| $$\frac{1}{3} \rightarrow$$  | $$\frac{4}{3} \rightarrow$$  | $$\frac{4}{5} \rightarrow$$  | $$\frac{7}{2} \rightarrow$$  |
|                              |                              |                              |                              |
| $$3$$                        | $$\frac{3}{4}$$              | $$\frac{5}{4}$$              | $$\frac{2}{7}$$              |
+==============================+==============================+==============================+==============================+
| e.                           | f.                           | g.                           | h.                           |
|                              |                              |                              |                              |
| $$\frac{3}{1} \rightarrow$$  | $$3 \rightarrow$$            | $$5 \rightarrow$$            | $$12 \rightarrow$$           |
|                              |                              |                              |                              |
| $$3$$                        | $$\frac{1}{3}$$              | $$\frac{1}{5}$$              | $$\frac{1}{12}$$             |
+------------------------------+------------------------------+------------------------------+------------------------------+
| i.                           | j.                           | k.                           | l.                           |
|                              |                              |                              |                              |
| $$\frac{3}{2} \rightarrow$$  | $$1\frac{1}{2} \rightarrow$$ | $$2\frac{1}{2} \rightarrow$$ | $$2\frac{3}{4} \rightarrow$$ |
|                              |                              |                              |                              |
| $$\frac{2}{3}$$              | $$\frac{2}{3}$$              | $$\frac{2}{5}$$              | $$\frac{4}{11}$$             |
+------------------------------+------------------------------+------------------------------+------------------------------+
| m.                           | n.                           | o.                           | p.                           |
|                              |                              |                              |                              |
| $$5\frac{3}{4} \rightarrow$$ | $$7 \rightarrow$$            | $$9\frac{2}{3} \rightarrow$$ | $$5\frac{5}{8} \rightarrow$$ |
|                              |                              |                              |                              |
| $$\frac{4}{23}$$             | $$\frac{1}{7}$$              | $$\frac{3}{29}$$             | $$\frac{8}{45}$$             |
